SELECT CASE
    WHEN EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM [Problems] AS [p]
        WHERE [p].[Id] = @__problemId_0) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END
2025-10-28 16:37:39.568 +05:30 [INF] Executed DbCommand (4ms) [Parameters=[@__problemId_0='?' (DbType = Int32)], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[ProblemId], [t].[Input], [t].[ExpectedOutput], COALESCE((
    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[Title]
    FROM [Problems] AS [p]
    WHERE [p].[Id] = [t].[ProblemId]), N'Unknown') AS [ProblemTitle]

    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[Id], [p].[Constraints], [p].[Description], [p].[Difficulty], [p].[Examples], [p].[Hints], [p].[MemoryLimit], [p].[SubdomainId], [p].[TimeLimit], [p].[Title]

    WHERE [p].[Id] = @__id_0
) AS [p0]
